 4 - Child is healthy/all right
 5 - Child is fit for immunization (i.e. DPT, Polio, etc.)

     for child's chest, throat, back or stomach

     etc.) be applied to affected area with or without kerosene or coconut oil

 3 - Exposed to sea breeze
 4 - Applied vaporub or ointment to child's chest, throat, back or stomach
 5 - Applied smoked/pounded atis or asiotes, mayana leaves to affected area
     (with or without kerosene or oil)
 6 - Applied kerosene, local vinegar or coconut oil on affected area
 7 - Other treatments (i.e. holy water)
 8 - Combination (SPECIFY)
 9 - Gave plenty of water
-8 - NR/DK
-9 - NA
